\DoxyCodeLine{02610\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02611\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NAME\ curl\_global\_sslset()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02612\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02613\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02614\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02615\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ built\ with\ multiple\ SSL\ backends,\ curl\_global\_sslset()\ allows\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02616\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ choose\ one.\ This\ function\ can\ only\ be\ called\ once,\ and\ it\ must\ be\ called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02617\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ *before*\ curl\_global\_init().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02618\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02619\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ backend\ can\ be\ identified\ by\ the\ id\ (e.g.\ CURLSSLBACKEND\_OPENSSL).\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02620\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ backend\ can\ also\ be\ specified\ via\ the\ name\ parameter\ (passing\ -\/1\ as\ id).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02621\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ both\ id\ and\ name\ are\ specified,\ the\ name\ will\ be\ ignored.\ If\ neither\ id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02622\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ nor\ name\ are\ specified,\ the\ function\ will\ fail\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02623\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CURLSSLSET\_UNKNOWN\_BACKEND\ and\ set\ the\ "{}avail"{}\ pointer\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02624\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NULL-\/terminated\ list\ of\ available\ backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02625\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02626\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Upon\ success,\ the\ function\ returns\ CURLSSLSET\_OK.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02627\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02628\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ the\ specified\ SSL\ backend\ is\ not\ available,\ the\ function\ returns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02629\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CURLSSLSET\_UNKNOWN\_BACKEND\ and\ sets\ the\ "{}avail"{}\ pointer\ to\ a\ NULL-\/terminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02630\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ list\ of\ available\ SSL\ backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02631\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02632\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ SSL\ backend\ can\ be\ set\ only\ once.\ If\ it\ has\ already\ been\ set,\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02633\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ subsequent\ attempt\ to\ change\ it\ will\ result\ in\ a\ CURLSSLSET\_TOO\_LATE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02634\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02635\ }
